       <p>
        Energetic, multi-talented and extremely versatile entertainers,
       </p>
       <p>
        with over 25 years of performance together,
       </p>
       <p>
        Private Stock is the most sought after entertainment in the industry.
       </p>
       <p>
        <span id="u21439-7">
         All performances are live, spontaneous, interactive and charged with positive energy!
        </span>
       </p>
       <p>
        The band
        <span id="u21439-10">
         can perform 4 hours or more with no band breaks.
        </span>
       </p>
       <p>
        All of our music is performed live, using wireless instruments and microphones,
       </p>
       <p>
        allowing us to move freely about the room.
       </p>
       <p>
        This provides your guests with a unique and interactive experience
       </p>
       <p>
        Whether you’re looking for a concert style show,  an elegant evening of entertainment
       </p>
       <p>
        with a touch of class, or a wild party with dancing all night long,
       </p>
       <p>
        Private Stock Band will make your next event memorable for all who attend!
